<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="211" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="218" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">plfa.Adequacy</a> <a id="232" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Introduction

Having proved a preservation property in the last chapter, a natural
next step would be to prove progress. That is, to prove a property
of the form

    If γ ⊢ M ↓ v, then either M is a lambda abstraction or M —→ N for some N.

Such a property would tell us that having a denotation implies either
reduction to normal form or divergence. This is indeed true, but we
can prove a much stronger property! In fact, having a denotation that
is a function value (not `⊥`) implies reduction to a lambda
abstraction (no divergence).

This stronger property, reformulated a bit, is known as _adequacy_.
That is, if a term `M` is denotationally equal to a lambda abstraction,
then `M` reduces to a lambda abstraction.

    ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)  implies M —↠ ƛ N' for some N'

Recall that `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)` is equivalent to saying that
`γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` for some `v` and `w`. We will show that
`γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies reduction a lambda abstraction.

It is well known that a term can reduce to a lambda abstraction using
full β reduction if and only if it can reduce to a lambda abstraction
using the call-by-name reduction strategy. So we shall prove that
`γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies that `M` halts under call-by-name evaluation,
which we define with a big-step semantics written `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c`, where
`c` is a closure (a term paired with an environment) and `γ'` is an
environment that maps variables to closures

So we will show that `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c`,
provided `γ` and `γ'` are appropriate related.  The proof will
be an induction on the derivation of `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, and to
strengthen the induction hypothesis, we will relate semantic values to
closures using a _logical relation_ `𝕍`.

The rest of this chapter is organized as follows.

* We loosen the requirement that `M` result in a function value and
  instead require that `M` result in a value that is greater than or
  equal to a function value. We establish several properties about
  being ``greater than a function''.

* We define the call-by-name big-step semantics of the lambda calculus
  and prove that it is deterministic.

* We define the logical relation `𝕍` that relates values and closures,
  and extend it to a relation on terms `𝔼` and environments `𝔾`.

* We prove the main lemma,
  that if `𝔾 γ γ'` and `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, then `𝔼 v (clos M γ')`.

* We prove adequacy as a corollary to the main lemma.

<a id="3759" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3764" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="3771" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html" class="Module">Data.Empty</a> <a id="3782" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="3788" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3789" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a><a id="3795" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3797" class="Keyword">renaming</a> <a id="3806" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3807" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">⊥</a> <a id="3809" class="Symbol">to</a> <a id="3812" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a><a id="3815" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="3817" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3822" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="3829" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Unit.html" class="Module">Data.Unit</a>

## The property of being greater or equal to a function

We define the following short-hand for saying that a value is
greather-than or equal to a function value.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun"></a><a id="4112" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3999" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4129" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4131" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="4135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4144" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4144" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4146" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4148" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="4151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4153" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="4155" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3999" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4161" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a> <a id="4163" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="4166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4166" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4168" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="4170" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3999" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4176" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a> <a id="4178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4031" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="4182" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4166" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4370" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="4186" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4144" class="Bound">u</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

If a value `u` is greater than a function, then an even greater value `u'`
is too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun-⊑"></a><a id="4297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4297" class="Function">AboveFun-⊑</a> <a id="4308" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4310" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="4312" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4312" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4314" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="4317" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4319" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3999" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="4324" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="4332" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4334" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4343" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4312" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4345" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4312" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4370" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="4351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4314" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
        <a id="4362" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
      <a id="4388" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4390" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4314" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

The bottom value `⊥` is not greater than a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun⊥"></a><a id="4547" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4547" class="Function">AboveFun⊥</a> <a id="4557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4559" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="4561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4019" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>
<a id="4572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4547" class="Function">AboveFun⊥</a> <a id="4582" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4584" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4584" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4586" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4588" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4590" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4590" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4592" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4594" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="4597" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4599" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>

    <a id="4716" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="4721" class="Bound">Γ⊆⊥</a> <a id="4725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4706" class="Bound">m</a>

If the join of two values `u` and `u'` is greater than a function, then
at least one of them is too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun-⊔"></a><a id="4863" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4863" class="Function">AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="4874" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4876" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="4878" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4878" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4880" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4880" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="4882" class="Symbol">}</a>
           <a id="4895" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4878" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4061" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4911" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4880" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="4913" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="4926" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4878" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4939" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#419" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="4941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4880" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

On the other hand, if neither of `u` and `u'` is greater than a function,
then their join is also not greater than a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-⊔"></a><a id="5375" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5375" class="Function">not-AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="5390" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5392" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="5394" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5394" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5396" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5396" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5399" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5401" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3999" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5406" class="Symbol">}</a>
               <a id="5423" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5425" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5427" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5436" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5394" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5438" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5440" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5442" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5396" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
               <a id="5469" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5471" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5473" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5394" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4061" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5396" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5489" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5375" class="Function">not-AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="5506" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5506" class="Bound">naf1</a> <a id="5511" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5511" class="Bound">naf2</a> <a id="5516" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5516" class="Bound">af12</a>
    <a id="5525" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="5530" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4863" class="Function">AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="5541" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5516" class="Bound">af12</a>
<a id="5546" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5550" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5552" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="5557" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5557" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5561" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5563" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5577" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5557" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5581" class="Bound">naf1</a>
<a id="5586" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5590" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5592" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="5597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5597" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5601" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5603" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5597" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5621" class="Bound">naf2</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The converse is also true. If the join of two values is not above a
function, then neither of them is individually.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-⊔-inv"></a><a id="5768" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5768" class="Function">not-AboveFun-⊔-inv</a> <a id="5787" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5789" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="5791" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5791" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5793" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5793" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5796" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3999" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5803" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5805" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5807" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5818" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5819" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5791" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4061" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5823" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5793" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5825" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="5841" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5843" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5791" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5856" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="5858" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5793" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

The property of being greater than a function value is decidable, as
exhibited by the following function.

## Relating values to closures

Next we relate semantic values to closures.  The relation `𝕍` is for
closures whose term is a lambda abstraction, i.e., in weak-head normal
form (WHNF). The relation 𝔼 is for any closure. Roughly speaking,
`𝔼 v c` will hold if, when `v` is greater than a function value, `c` evaluates
to a closure `c'` in WHNF and `𝕍 v c'`. Regarding `𝕍 v c`, it will hold when
`c` is in WHNF, and if `v` is a function, the body of `c` evaluates
according to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝕍"></a><a id="7222" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7224" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7226" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3999" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="7232" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7234" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2629" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7239" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7241" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="𝔼"></a><a id="7245" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7245" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="7247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3999" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="7255" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2629" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7262" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7264" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We define `𝕍` as a function from values and closures to `Set` and not as a
data type because it is mutually recursive with `𝔼` in a negative
position (to the left of an implication).  We first perform case
analysis on the term in the closure. If the term is a variable or
application, then `𝕍` is false (`Bot`). If the term is a lambda
abstraction, we define `𝕍` by recursion on the value, which we
describe below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7709" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7711" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7713" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7719" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="7722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7722" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7724" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7726" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7726" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7727" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7729" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7731" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a>
<a id="7735" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7737" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7737" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7739" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7740" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7746" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7748" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="7750" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7750" class="Bound">M₁</a><a id="7752" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7754" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7754" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7755" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7757" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7759" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a>

    <a id="7817" class="Symbol">(∀{</a><a id="7820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7820" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="7822" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7824" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2629" class="Datatype">Clos</a><a id="7828" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7830" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7832" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7245" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="7834" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7789" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7836" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7820" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="7838" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7840" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="7849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7793" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7851" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7853" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="7856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7856" class="Bound">c&#39;</a> <a id="7859" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="7861" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2629" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7866" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a>
        <a id="7876" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7877" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7808" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="7879" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2850" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="7882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7820" class="Bound">c</a><a id="7883" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7885" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3215" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7805" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="7889" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3215" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="7891" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7856" class="Bound">c&#39;</a>  <a id="7895" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a>  <a id="7898" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7900" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7793" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7856" class="Bound">c&#39;</a><a id="7904" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7906" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7908" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7909" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="7911" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4061" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="7913" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7913" class="Bound">v</a><a id="7914" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7916" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7917" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7922" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7925" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7926" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7928" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7929" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7931" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7935" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7909" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="7937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7938" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7943" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7944" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7946" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7925" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7947" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7949" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7928" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7950" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7952" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="7954" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7956" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7913" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7959" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7964" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7965" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7925" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7968" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7928" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7971" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* If the value is `⊥`, then the result is true (`⊤`).

* If the value is a join (u ⊔ v), then the result is the pair
  (conjunction) of 𝕍 is true for both u and v.

* The important case is for a function value `v ↦ w` and closure
  `clos (ƛ N) γ`. Given any closure `c` such that `𝔼 v c`, if `w` is
  greater than a function, then `N` evaluates (with `γ` extended with `c`)
  to some closure `c'` and we have `𝕍 w c'`.


The definition of `𝔼` is straightforward. If `v` is a greater than a
function, then `M` evaluates to a closure related to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="8547" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7245" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="8549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8549" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8551" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8559" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="8561" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8563" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8565" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="8574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8549" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8576" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8578" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="8581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8581" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8583" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="8585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2629" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="8590" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a> <a id="8592" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8559" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="8595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3215" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="8597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8557" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="8599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3215" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="8601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8581" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8603" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="8605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="8607" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8549" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8581" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the main lemma is by induction on `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, so it goes
underneath lambda abstractions and must therefore reason about open
terms (terms with variables). So we must relate environments of
semantic values to environments of closures.  In the following, `𝔾`
relates `γ` to `γ'` if the corresponding values and closures are related
by `𝔼`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝔾"></a><a id="8989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8989" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="8991" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8993" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8995" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="8996" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8998" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9000" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7233" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="9004" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8995" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9006" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9008" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2599" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="9016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8995" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9018" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9020" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="9024" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8989" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9026" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9027" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9028" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9030" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9030" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9032" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9035" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9037" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9039" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9041" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9027" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9045" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="9047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9048" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9050" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7245" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="9054" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9030" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9057" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9039" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9058" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9060" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9032" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9039" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9065" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="𝔾-∅"></a><a id="9068" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9068" class="Function">𝔾-∅</a> <a id="9072" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9074" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8989" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7373" class="Function">`∅</a> <a id="9079" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2828" class="Function">∅&#39;</a>

      <a id="9143" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9145" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8989" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9105" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9116" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9152" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7245" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="9156" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9132" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9158" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9134" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9160" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8989" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9164" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9165" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9105" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9167" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7406" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="9170" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9132" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9171" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9173" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9174" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9116" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9177" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2850" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="9180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9134" class="Bound">c</a><a id="9181" class="Symbol">)</a>

We need a few properties of the `𝕍` and `𝔼` relations.  The first is that
a closure in the `𝕍` relation must be in weak-head normal form.  We
define WHNF has follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9441" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="WHNF"></a><a id="9446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9446" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9451" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9453" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9455" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9456" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9458" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9459" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9461" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9463" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9456" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9465" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9458" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9469" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9471" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="9475" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="WHNF.ƛ_"></a><a id="9483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9483" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="9486" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9488" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9490" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9491" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9492" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9494" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9495" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9495" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="9497" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9491" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="9505" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9508" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="9515" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9517" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9446" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9522" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9523" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="9525" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9495" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9526" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof goes by cases on the term in the closure.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝕍→WHNF"></a><a id="9606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9606" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9613" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9615" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9617" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9618" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9620" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9622" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9624" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2599" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="9632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9617" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9633" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9635" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9635" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="9637" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9617" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9644" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9646" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9647" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="9656" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9646" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9662" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9663" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9668" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9635" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="9670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9620" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="9671" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9673" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9675" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9446" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9680" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9635" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="9682" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9606" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9689" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9690" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9692" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="9696" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9696" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9697" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9699" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9700" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9700" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9701" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9703" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="9706" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9606" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9713" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9714" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9716" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="9720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9720" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9721" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9723" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9724" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9725" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9727" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="9730" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9732" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9483" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a>
<a id="9735" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9606" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9742" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9743" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9745" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9747" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="9749" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="9751" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9751" class="Bound">M</a><a id="9752" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9754" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9755" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9756" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9758" class="Symbol">()</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Next we have an introduction rule for `𝕍` that mimics the `⊔-intro`
rule. If both `u` and `v` are related to a closure `c`, then their join is
too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝕍⊔-intro"></a><a id="9935" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9935" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="9944" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9946" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9948" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9948" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9950" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9952" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9952" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9953" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="9964" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9968" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9950" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9948" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9972" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9974" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9952" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9948" class="Bound">c</a>
           <a id="9991" class="Comment">---------------</a>
         <a id="10016" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="10020" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9950" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="10023" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4061" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9952" class="Bound">v</a><a id="10026" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10028" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9948" class="Bound">c</a>
<a id="10030" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9935" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10039" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10040" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10045" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="10048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10048" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10049" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10051" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10052" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10054" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="10057" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10057" class="Bound">vc</a>
<a id="10060" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9935" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10069" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10070" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10075" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10078" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10078" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10079" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10081" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10082" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10084" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="10087" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10087" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="10090" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10092" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="10094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10084" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="10097" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10087" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="10102" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="10104" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9935" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10113" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10119" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10120" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10120" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="10122" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10124" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10124" class="Bound">M</a><a id="10125" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10127" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10127" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10128" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10130" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="10133" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10133" class="Bound">vc</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In a moment we prove that `𝕍` is preserved when going from a greater
value to a lesser value: if `𝕍 v c` and `v' ⊑ v`, then `𝕍 v' c`.
This property, named `𝕍-sub`, is needed by the main lemma in
the case for the `sub` rule.

To prove `𝕍-sub`, we in turn need the following property concerning
values that are not greater than a function, that is, values that are
equivalent to `⊥`. In such cases, `𝕍 v (clos (ƛ N) γ')` is trivially true.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-𝕍"></a><a id="10600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10600" class="Function">not-AboveFun-𝕍</a> <a id="10615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10617" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="10619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10619" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10621" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3999" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="10628" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10630" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10630" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="10631" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10633" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="10636" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2599" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="10646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10630" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="10647" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10649" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="10651" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10630" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10657" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="10659" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="10661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="10663" class="Symbol">}</a>

      <a id="10690" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
    <a id="10714" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10716" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7222" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="10718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10619" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10720" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10721" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10726" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10649" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10730" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10732" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10633" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="10734" class="Symbol">)</a>

The proofs of `𝕍-sub` and `𝔼-sub` are intertwined.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sub-𝕍"></a><a id="11043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11043" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="11049" endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4370" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="11136" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11115" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11138" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7245" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="11142" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11117" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="11145" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11105" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We prove `𝕍-sub` by case analysis on the closure's term, to dispatch the
cases for variables and application. We then proceed by induction on
`v' ⊑ v`. We describe each case below.

    <a id="12899" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="12904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4863" class="Function">AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="12915" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="12917" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12851" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="12920" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12922" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="12924" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12858" class="Bound">w&#39;&#39;</a> <a id="12928" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12930" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12864" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="12933" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="12935" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="12937" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="12941" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="12943" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="12948" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12948" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="12952" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12954" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="12961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12962" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="12976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12948" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="12980" class="Bound">naf2</a><a id="12984" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12986" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="12990" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="12992" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="12997" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12997" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="13001" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13003" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="13010" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13011" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="13025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12997" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="13029" class="Bound">naf3</a><a id="13033" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `Bot⊑`. We immediately have `𝕍 ⊥ (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `ConjL⊑`.

        v₁' ⊑ v     v₂' ⊑ v
        -------------------
        (v₁' ⊔ v₂') ⊑ v

  The induction hypotheses gives us `𝕍 v₁' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`
  and `𝕍 v₂' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`, which is all we need for this case.

* Case `ConjR1⊑`.

        v' ⊑ v₁
        -------------
        v' ⊑ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)

  The induction hypothesis gives us `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `ConjR2⊑`.

        v' ⊑ v₂
        -------------
        v' ⊑ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)

  Again, the induction hypothesis gives us `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `Trans⊑`.

        v' ⊑ v₂   v₂ ⊑ v
        -----------------
             v' ⊑ v

  The induction hypothesis for `v₂ ⊑ v` gives us
  `𝕍 v₂ (clos (ƛ N) γ)`. We apply the induction hypothesis
  for `v' ⊑ v₂` to conclude that `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `Dist⊑`. This case  is the most difficult. We have

        𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ)
        𝕍 (v ↦ w') (clos (ƛ N) γ)

  and need to show that

        𝕍 (v ↦ (w ⊔ w')) (clos (ƛ N) γ)

  Let `c` be an arbtrary closure such that `𝔼 v c`.
  Assume `w ⊔ w'` is greater than a function.
  Unfortunately, this does not mean that both `w` and `w'`
  are above functions. But thanks to the lemma `AboveFun-⊔`,
  we know that at least one of them is greater than a function.

  * Suppose both of them are greater than a function.  Then we have
    `γ ⊢ N ⇓ clos L δ` and `𝕍 w (clos L δ)`.  We also have `γ ⊢ N ⇓ c₃` and
    `𝕍 w' c₃`.  Because the big-step semantics is deterministic, we have
    `c₃ ≡ clos L δ`. Also, from `𝕍 w (clos L δ)` we know that `L ≡ ƛ N'`
    for some `N'`. We conclude that `𝕍 (w ⊔ w') (clos (ƛ N') δ)`.

  * Suppose one of them is greater than a function and the other is
    not: say `AboveFun w` and `¬ AboveFun w'`. Then from
    `𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ)`
    we have `γ ⊢ N ⇓ clos L γ₁` and `𝕍 w (clos L γ₁)`. From this we have
    `L ≡ ƛ N'` for some `N'`. Meanwhile, from `¬ AboveFun w'` we have
    `𝕍 w' (clos L γ₁)`. We conclude that
    `𝕍 (w ⊔ w') (clos (ƛ N') γ₁)`.


The proof of `sub-𝔼` is direct and explained below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11095" class="Function">sub-𝔼</a> <a id="15156" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15157" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="15162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15162" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="15164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15164" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="15165" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15167" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15168" class="Bound">v</a><a id="15169" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15171" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15172" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="15174" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15176" class="Bound">𝔼v</a> <a id="15179" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15179" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="15184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15184" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a>
    <a id="15192" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="15197" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15176" class="Bound">𝔼v</a> <a id="15200" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15201" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4297" class="Function">AboveFun-⊑</a> <a id="15212" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15184" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="15216" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15179" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a><a id="15220" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15222" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="15226" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="15228" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15230" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15230" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="15232" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15234" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15236" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15236" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="15240" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15242" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="15245" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15247" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15249" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="15257" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15259" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15230" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="15261" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15263" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15265" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15236" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="15269" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15271" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11043" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="15277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15242" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="15280" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="15285" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15287" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

From `AboveFun v'` and `v' ⊑ v` we have `AboveFun v`.  Then with `𝔼 v c` we
obtain a closure `c` such that `γ ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v c`. We conclude with an
application of `sub-𝕍` with `v' ⊑ v` to show `𝕍 v' c`.


## Programs with function denotation terminate via call-by-name

The main lemma proves that if a term has a denotation that is above a
function, then it terminates via call-by-name. More formally, if
`γ ⊢ M ↓ v` and `𝔾 γ γ'`, then `𝔼 v (clos M γ')`. The proof is by
induction on the derivation of `γ ⊢ M ↓ v` we discuss each case below.

The following lemma, kth-x, is used in the case for the `var` rule.

      <a id="18282" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18284" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18255" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="18286" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18288" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18290" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18261" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="18294" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18296" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11043" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="18302" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18267" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="18305" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="18310" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="18312" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `var`. Looking up `x` in `γ'` yields some closure, `clos M' δ`,
  and from `𝔾 γ γ'` we have `𝔼 (γ x) (clos M' δ)`. With the premise
  `AboveFun (γ x)`, we obtain a closure `c` such that `δ ⊢ M' ⇓ c`
  and `𝕍 (γ x) c`. To conclude `γ' ⊢ x ⇓ c` via `⇓-var`, we
  need `γ' x ≡ clos M' δ`, which is obvious, but it requires some
  Agda shananigans via the `kth-x` lemma to get our hands on it.

* Case `↦-elim`. We have `γ ⊢ L · M ↓ v`.
  The induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ L ↓ v₁ ↦ v`
  gives us `γ' ⊢ L ⇓ clos L' δ` and `𝕍 v (clos L' δ)`.
  Of course, `L' ≡ ƛ N` for some `N`.
  By the induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁`,
  we have `𝔼 v₁ (clos M γ')`.
  Together with the premise `AboveFun v` and `𝕍 v (clos L' δ)`,
  we obtain a closure `c'` such that `δ ⊢ N ⇓ c'` and `𝕍 v c'`.
  We conclude that `γ' ⊢ L · M ⇓ c'` by rule `⇓-app`.

* Case `↦-intro`. We have `γ ⊢ ƛ N ↓ v ↦ w`.
  We immediately have `γ' ⊢ ƛ M ⇓ clos (ƛ M) γ'` by rule `⇓-lam`.
  But we also need to prove `𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ')`.
  Let `c` by an arbitrary closure such that `𝔼 v c`.
  Suppose `v'` is greater than a function value.
  We need to show that `γ' , c ⊢ N ⇓ c'` and `𝕍 v' c'` for some `c'`.
  We prove this by the induction hypothesis for `γ , v ⊢ N ↓ v'`
  but we must first show that `𝔾 (γ , v) (γ' , c)`. We prove
  that by the lemma `𝔾-ext`, using facts `𝔾 γ γ'` and `𝔼 v c`.

* Case `⊥-intro`. We have the premise `AboveFun ⊥`, but that's impossible.

* Case `⊔-intro`. We have `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)` and `AboveFun (v₁ ⊔ v₂)`
  and need to show `γ' ⊢ M ↓ c` and `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) c` for some `c`.
  Again, by `AboveFun-⊔`, at least one of `v₁` or `v₂` is greater than
  a function.

  * Suppose both `v₁` and `v₂` are greater than a function value.
    By the induction hypotheses for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁` and `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₂`
    we have `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c₁`, `𝕍 v₁ c₁`, `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c₂`, and `𝕍 v₂ c₂`
    for some `c₁` and `c₂`. Because `⇓` is deterministic, we have `c₂ ≡ c₁`.
    Then by `𝕍⊔-intro` we conclude that `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) c₁`.

  * Without loss of generality, suppose `v₁` is greater than a function
    value but `v₂` is not.  By the induction hypotheses for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁`,
    and using `𝕍→WHNF`, we have `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N) γ₁`
    and `𝕍 v₁ (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`.
    Then because `v₂` is not greater than a function, we also have
    `𝕍 v₂ (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`. We conclude that `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`.

* Case `sub`. We have `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, `v' ⊑ v`, and `AboveFun v'`.
  We need to show that `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v' c` for some `c`.
  We have `AboveFun v` by `AboveFun-⊑`,
  so the induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v` gives us a closure `c`
  such that `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v c`. We conclude that `𝕍 v' c` by `sub-𝕍`.


## Proof of denotational adequacy

The adequacy property is a corollary of the main lemma.
We have `∅ ⊢ ƛ N ↓ ⊥ ↦ ⊥`, so `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)`
gives us `∅ ⊢ M ↓ ⊥ ↦ ⊥`. Then the main lemma gives us
`∅ ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) γ` for some `N′` and `γ`.

            <a id="21417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2828" class="Function">∅&#39;</a> <a id="21420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3215" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="21422" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21291" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="21424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3215" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="21426" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="21431" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="21434" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21367" class="Bound">N′</a><a id="21436" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21438" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21389" class="Bound">γ</a>

    <a id="21601" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="21606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9606" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="21613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21590" class="Bound">Vc</a>

## Call-by-name is equivalent to beta reduction

As promised, we return to the question of whether call-by-name
evaluation is equivalent to beta reduction. In the chapter CallByName
we established the forward direction: that if call-by-name produces a
result, then the program beta reduces to a lambda abstraction.  We now
prove the backward direction of the if-and-only-if, leveraging our
results about the denotational semantics.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="reduce→cbn"></a><a id="22129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22129" class="Function">reduce→cbn</a> <a id="22140" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22142" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22144" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22145" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22145" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22147" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="22151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="22154" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22156" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22157" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22157" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="22159" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22161" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="22163" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="22165" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="22167" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22169" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="22170" class="Symbol">}</a>
           <a id="22183" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22145" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22187" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/LambdaReduction.md %}{% raw %}#894" class="Datatype Operator">—↠</a> <a id="22190" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22157" class="Bound">N</a>

             <a id="22276" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2828" class="Function">∅&#39;</a> <a id="22279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3215" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22281" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22145" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3215" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="22285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2648" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="22290" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22291" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22293" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22227" class="Bound">N′</a><a id="22295" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22247" class="Bound">δ</a>
<a id="22299" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22129" class="Function">reduce→cbn</a> <a id="22310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22310" class="Bound">M—↠ƛN</a> <a id="22316" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22318" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21278" class="Function">adequacy</a> <a id="22327" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22328" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#23798" class="Function">soundness</a> <a id="22338" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22310" class="Bound">M—↠ƛN</a><a id="22343" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Suppose `M —↠ ƛ N`. Soundness of the denotational semantics gives us
`ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)`. Then by adequacy we conclude that
`∅' ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) δ` for some `N′` and `δ`.

Putting the two directions of the if-and-only-if together, we
establish that call-by-name evaluation is equivalent to beta reduction
in the following sense.
